Script1.Name = "Script1"
Script1.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script1.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script1.Position = UDim2.new(0.0127737224, 0, 0.0437499993, 0)
Script1.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script1.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script1.Text = "Autotime"
Script1.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script1.TextSize = 26.000
Script1.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	local uis = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local rblx_connection = nil
	local hm = function()
		if player.Character:FindFirstChild("ball.weld") then
			player.Character.LowerTorso.MainGui.Shooting.Bar:TweenSize(UDim2.new(.5, 0, 1, 0), "Out", "Linear", 0, true)
		end
	end

	uis.InputBegan:Connect(function(key, gpe)
		if gpe then return end
		if key.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.E then
			rblx_connection = game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:Connect(hm)
		end
	end)

	uis.InputEnded:Connect(function(key, gpe)
		if gpe then return end

		if key.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.E then
			rblx_connection:Disconnect()
			rblx_connection = nil
			repeat wait()
				player.Character.LowerTorso.MainGui.Shooting.Bar:TweenSize(UDim2.new(.5, 0, 1, 0), "Out", "Linear", 0, true)
			until not player.Character:FindFirstChild("ball.weld")
			wait(0.5)
			player.Character.LowerTorso.MainGui.Shooting.Bar:TweenSize(UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0), "Out", "Linear", 0, true)
		end
	end)
end)

Script3.Name = "Script3"
Script3.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script3.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script3.Position = UDim2.new(0.666058362, 0, 0.0437499993, 0)
Script3.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script3.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script3.Text = "AutoDB"
Script3.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script3.TextSize = 26.000
Script3.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
		Title = "AUTO DROPBALL ACTIVATED";
		Text = "Press L to turn off and on.";
	})

	local UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local bool = true


	UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp, gpe)
		if gpe then return end

		if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.L then 
			bool = not bool
			print("looping ended")
		end
	end)

	while wait() do 
		if bool then 
			local descendants = game.workspace:GetDescendants()

			for index, descendants in pairs(descendants) do
				if descendants .Name == "Basketball" then
					descendants.block:FireServer()


				end
			end
		end
	end
end)

Script5.Text = "OpStat"
Script5.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script5.TextSize = 26.000
Script5.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	for i,v in pairs(getgc(true)) do
		if type(v) == "table" and rawget(v, "handles") then
			v.freethrow = 99;
			v.postscorer = 99;
			v.ballspeed = 99;
			v.jump = 99;
			v.steal = 99;
			v.shotcontest = 99;
			v["2pointer"] = 99;
			v["3pointer"] = 99;
			v.passing = 99;
			v.layup = 99;
			v.strength = 99;
			v.dunk = 99;
			v.speed = 99;
			v.handles = 99;
			v.movingshot = 99;
			v.defense = 99;
			v.stamina = 99;
		end
	end
end)

Script7.Name = "Script7"
Script7.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script7.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script7.Position = UDim2.new(0.0127737522, 0, 0.49999997, 0)
Script7.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script7.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script7.Text = "ArmExtend"
Script7.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script7.TextSize = 26.000
Script7.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Press k to toggle", Text = "Script made by CodedStudio#9755"})

	_G.Resized = true
	local Player = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
	local Mouse = Player:GetMouse()

	Mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(Key)
		if Key == 'k' then
			_G.Resized = not _G.Resized
			if _G.Resized == true then
				Player.Character['LeftHand'].Size = Vector3.new(1, 10, 1)
				Player.Character['RightHand'].Size = Vector3.new(1, 10, 1)
			elseif _G.Resized == false then
				Player.Character['LeftHand'].Size = Vector3.new(0.69334, 1.10182, 0.744331)
				Player.Character['RightHand'].Size = Vector3.new(0.69334, 1.10182, 0.744331)
			end
		end
	end)
end)

Script9.Name = "Script9"
Script9.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script9.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script9.Position = UDim2.new(0.666058421, 0, 0.49999997, 0)
Script9.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script9.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script9.Text = "NoClip"
Script9.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script9.TextSize = 26.000
Script9.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Hold v to noclip!", Text = "Script Executed!!"})


	local h,char,play
	play = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local uis = game:getService("UserInputService")
	game:getService("RunService"):BindToRenderStep("",0,function()
		char = play.Character
		if char then h = char:findFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") end
		if not h then return end
		if uis:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.V) then
			h:ChangeState(11)
		end
	end)
end)

Script10.Name = "Script10"
Script10.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script10.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script10.Position = UDim2.new(0.0127737522, 0, 0.737500012, 0)
Script10.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script10.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script10.Text = "Teleport"
Script10.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script10.TextSize = 26.000
Script10.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer

	hum = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart

	mouse = plr:GetMouse()



	mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)

		if key == "b" then

			if mouse.Target then

				hum.CFrame = CFrame.new(mouse.Hit.x, mouse.Hit.y + 5, mouse.Hit.z)

			end

		end
	end)
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
		Title = "GG!";
		Text = "Teleport Activated!; Press Q to teleport!";
	})
end)

Script12.Name = "Script12"
Script12.Parent = ScriptFrame
Script12.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
Script12.Position = UDim2.new(0.666058421, 0, 0.737500012, 0)
Script12.Size = UDim2.new(0, 173, 0, 56)
Script12.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
Script12.Text = "Credits:"
Script12.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
Script12.TextSize = 26.000
Script12.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Script by:", Text = "Main#5026"})
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Gui dsfx:", Text = "Main#5026"})
	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Functions", Text = "Main#5026"})
end)

local uis = game:GetService("UserInputService")

uis.InputBegan:Connect(function(i)
 if i.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.RightShift then
   if MainFrame.Visible == false then
    MainFrame.Visible = true
else
    MainFrame.Visible = false
end
end
end)
